<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разрешать.html>разреша́ть</a> (5059)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:решать.html>реша́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rešátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрешать.html>разреша́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razrešátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрешить.html>разреши́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to permit, to allow</li>
<li>to solve, to resolve</li>
<li>to authorize</li>
<li>to settle (<i>a problem</i>)</li></ol>

***разрешаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разрешаться.html>разреша́ться</a> (8597)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрешать.html>разреша́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razrešátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрешаться.html>разреша́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razrešátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрешиться.html>разреши́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be solved</li>
<li>to be settled/resolved</li>
<li>to be allowed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здесь.html>здесь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:курить.html>кури́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разрешаться.html>разреша́ется</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zdesʹ kurítʹ ne <b>razrešájetsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">no smoking (is allowed) here</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрешать.html>разреша́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razrešátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрешение.html>разреше́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razrešénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разрешить.html>разреши́ть</a> (1413)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:решить.html>реши́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rešítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрешить.html>разреши́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razrešítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрешать.html>разреша́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to permit, to allow, to let</li>
<li>to authorize</li>
<li>to solve, to settle, to resolve</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разрешиться.html>разреши́ться</a> (20800)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрешить.html>разреши́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razrešítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрешиться.html>разреши́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razrešítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрешаться.html>разреша́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be solved</li>
<li>to be settled/resolved</li>
<li>to be allowed</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрешить.html>разреши́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razrešítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***разрушать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разрушать.html>разруша́ть</a> (6639)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрушить.html>разру́шить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razrúšitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрушать.html>разруша́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razrušátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрушить.html>разру́шить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to destroy, to demolish, to wreck</li>
<li>to ruin</li>
<li>to frustrate, to blast, to blight, to wreck</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разрушаться.html>разруша́ться</a> (16228)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрушать.html>разруша́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razrušátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разрушение.html>разруше́ние</a> (5280)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрушить.html>разру́шить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razrúšitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрушение.html>разруше́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razrušénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрушение.html>разруше́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрушение.html>разруше́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрушение.html>разруше́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>destruction, demolition, devastation (the act of destroying)</li></ol>

***разрушить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разрушить.html>разру́шить</a> (3291)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рушить.html>ру́шить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rúšitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрушить.html>разру́шить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razrúšitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрушать.html>разруша́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to destroy, to demolish, to wreck</li>
<li>to ruin</li>
<li>to frustrate, to blast, to blight, to wreck</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрушить.html>разру́шить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razrúšitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разрыв.html>разры́в</a> (3012)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрыв.html>разры́в</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razrýv</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрыв.html>разры́ва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрыв.html>разры́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрыв.html>разры́вов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rupture</li>
<li>explosion</li>
<li>break, gap</li></ol>

***разрываться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разрываться.html>разрыва́ться</a> (12800)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрывать.html>разрыва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрываться.html>разрыва́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razryvátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разорваться.html>разорва́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to break, to tear, to burst
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>се́рдце</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разрываться.html>разрыва́ется</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó sérdce <b>razryvájetsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">his heart is breaking</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to burst, to go off, to explode</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to struggle to do (cope with) everything at once
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разрываться.html>разрыва́ться</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on ne móžet <b>razryvátʹsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he can't be everywhere at once</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрывать.html>разрыва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрывать.html>разрыва́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razryvájuščij</span>)

***разряд.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разряд.html>разря́д</a> (4539)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разряд.html>разря́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razrjád</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разряд.html>разря́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разряд.html>разря́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разряд.html>разря́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>category, class</li>
<li>discharge</li>
<li>unloading</li>
<li>numerical place, digit</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разрядить.html>разряди́ть</a> (15000)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрядить.html>разряди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razrjadítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">разряжа́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to discharge (battery)</li>
<li>to ease (tensions)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрядить.html>разряди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razrjadítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">разряжа́ть</b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрядить.html>разряди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razrjadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрядка.html>разря́дка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razrjádka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрядка.html>разря́дки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрядка.html>разря́дки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрядка.html>разря́док</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">electricity</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> discharge</li>
<li><i>(of weapon)</i> discharge, unloading</li>
<li>relaxation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разрядка.html>разря́дка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:международный.html>междунаро́дной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:напряженность.html>напряжённости</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razrjádka</b> meždunaródnoj naprjažónnosti</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">relaxation/lessening of international tension; détente</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хоро́шая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разрядка.html>разря́дка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éto xoróšaja <b>razrjádka</b> dlja menjá</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">this is a good way for me to relax</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">polygraphy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> spacing</li></ol>
